Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Reversing the system.
Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 9-rules system (6 strict rules).
Removing 3 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 6-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 95-rules system (11 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 90-rules system (11 strict rules).
Removing 2 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 88-rules system (11 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 5 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 87-rules system (10 strict rules).

Remains to prove termination of a 86-rules system (9 strict rules).

Remains to prove termination of a 396-rules system (0 strict rules).

Proof:

After renaming modulo the bijection { a ↦ 0, b ↦ 1, c ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ 1 2 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 2 0 ,
  2 2 2 ⟶ 0 1 }

Reversing the system.
After renaming modulo the bijection { 0 ↦ 0, 2 ↦ 1, 1 ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ 1 2 ,
  2 0 ⟶ 0 1 ,
  1 1 1 ⟶ 2 0 }

Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
  Here, ↑ marks so-called defined symbols.
After renaming modulo the bijection { (0,↑) ↦ 0, (1,↑) ↦ 1, (2,↓) ↦ 2, (2,↑) ↦ 3, (0,↓) ↦ 4, (1,↓) ↦ 5 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 9-rules system (6 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ 1 2 ,
  0 ⟶ 3 ,
  3 4 ⟶ 0 5 ,
  3 4 ⟶ 1 ,
  1 5 5 ⟶ 3 4 ,
  1 5 5 ⟶ 0 ,
  4 →= 5 2 ,
  2 4 →= 4 5 ,
  5 5 5 →= 2 4 }
